		<Enumeration Name="GrbCh0TrigCfgContinuousPipeCount">
			<ToolTip>Controls the number of GigE Vision blocks (frames) that can be in the acquisition and transfer pipe.</ToolTip>
			<Description>Controls the number of GigE Vision blocks (frames) that can be in the acquisition and transfer pipe. A frame is considered to be in the pipe from the moment it starts until its last packet is transmitted on the Ethernet link. When the specified number of frames is reached, the IP engine ignores any new frames from the camera head until the number of frames in the pipe decreases. In continuous pipe count or recording acquisition modes, the limit is set by the amount of onboard memory available in the IP engine, rather than the number of frames in the pipe. The IP engine acquires frames from the camera until the memory is filled up to the water-level setting (GrbCh0AcqCfgMemoryWaterLevel).</Description>
			<DisplayName>Acquisition and Transfer Pipe Mode</DisplayName>
			<Visibility>Beginner</Visibility>
			<pIsLocked>TLParamsLocked</pIsLocked>
			<Streamable>Yes</Streamable>
			<EnumEntry Name="Continuous"><Value>0</Value></EnumEntry>
			<EnumEntry Name="One"><Value>1</Value></EnumEntry>
			<EnumEntry Name="Two"><Value>2</Value></EnumEntry>
			<pValue>GrbCh0TrigCfgContinuousPipeCountReg</pValue>
